**GT:** `-0.0585985712804097*v**3 - 0.716668620096812*v - 0.358334310048406*v*exp(-Abs(v)) + 0.66863216766915*sin(t)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `v**3` term
2. `v` term (linear)
3. `v*exp(-Abs(v))` term
4. `sin(t)` term

No dependence on `x` at all. Let me check each candidate.

**Key observation:** The GT has NO dependence on `x`. Any candidate with `x`-dependent terms that cannot be zeroed out will not match. Also, the GT has a `v*exp(-Abs(v))` term, which is a very specific nonlinear function of `v`.

Let me systematically go through candidates:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x/(c1 + x**2) + c2*v/(c3 + Abs(v)) + c4 + c5*cos(c6*t + c7) + c8*v/sqrt(c9 + v**2)`
- Set c0=0 to kill x-dependence. Remaining: `c2*v/(c3 + Abs(v)) + c4 + c5*cos(c6*t + c7) + c8*v/sqrt(c9 + v**2)`
- The `sin(t)` can be matched by `cos(t + c7)` with c7 = -π/2.
- But we need `v**3`, `v`, and `v*exp(-Abs(v))`. The candidate has `v/(c3 + Abs(v))` and `v/sqrt(c9 + v**2)` — these are rational/algebraic functions of v, not polynomial or exponential. They cannot produce `v**3` or `v*exp(-Abs(v))`.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0 + c1*exp(c2*x) + c3*x**3 + c4*x + c5*v*Abs(v) + c6*v + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)`
- Set c1=0, c3=0, c4=0 to kill x-dependence. Remaining: `c0 + c5*v*Abs(v) + c6*v + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)`
- Has `v*Abs(v)` (which equals `v*|v|`, not `v**3`) and `v`, `cos` (→ sin), constant.
- GT needs `v**3` and `v*exp(-Abs(v))`. `v*|v| = sign(v)*v**2 ≠ v**3`. Missing `v**3` and `v*exp(-Abs(v))`.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*v + c3*v*Abs(v) + c4*x**c5*exp(c6*x) + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)`
- Set c0=0, c4=0 to kill x. Remaining: `c1 + c2*v + c3*v*Abs(v) + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)`
- Missing `v**3` and `v*exp(-Abs(v))`.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `c0*x/(c1 + x**2) + c2*v/(c3 + Abs(v)) + c4 + c5*cos(c6*t + c7) + c8*v*exp(c9*x)`
- Set c0=0, c8=0 (or c9=0 gives c8*v which is just linear v). With c9=0: `c2*v/(c3+|v|) + c4 + c5*cos(...) + c8*v`
- Missing `v**3` and `v*exp(-Abs(v))`.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `c0*exp(c1*x) + c2 + c3*exp(c4*x)/x**5 + c5*v/(c6 + Abs(v)) + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)`
- x terms can't all be zeroed easily (c3*exp(c4*x)/x**5 can't be zero unless c3=0). Set c0=0, c3=0. Remaining: `c2 + c5*v/(c6+|v|) + c7*cos(...)`. Missing key terms.
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** `c0 + c1*exp(c2*x) + c3*x**3 + c4*x + c5*v*Abs(v) + c6*cos(c7*t + c8)`
- Set c1=0, c3=0, c4=0. Remaining: `c0 + c5*v*|v| + c6*cos(...)`. Missing `v**3`, `v`, `v*exp(-|v|)`.
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** `c0 + c1*exp(c2*x) + c3*v + c4*v**3 + c5*sin(c6*t + c7) + c8*v*exp(c9*v**2)`
- Set c1=0 to kill x. Remaining: `c0 + c3*v + c4*v**3 + c5*sin(c6*t + c7) + c8*v*exp(c9*v**2)`
- Has `v**3`, `v`, `sin(t)` (with c6=1, c7=0). Has `v*exp(c9*v**2)`.
- GT needs `v*exp(-|v|)`. Can `v*exp(c9*v**2)` equal `v*exp(-|v|)`? That would need `c9*v**2 = -|v|`, i.e., `c9*|v| = -1` for all v, impossible.
Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 8:** `c0*x**3 + c1*x**2 + c2*v**3 + c3*v + c4*x + c5 + c6*cos(c7*t + c8) + c9*v*Abs(v)`
- Set c0=0, c1=0, c4=0. Remaining: `c2*v**3 + c3*v + c5 + c6*cos(c7*t+c8) + c9*v*|v|`
- Has `v**3`, `v`, `cos→sin`, `v*|v|`. But GT needs `v*exp(-|v|)`, not `v*|v|`.
- `v*|v|` is NOT equivalent to `v*exp(-|v|)`. These are fundamentally different functions.
Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 9:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*v**3 + c5*v`
- Set c0=0. Remaining: `c1 + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*v**3 + c5*v`
- Has `exp(c3*t)` instead of `sin(t)`. These are not equivalent. Missing `v*exp(-|v|)`.
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10:** `c0*x**3 + c1*x**2 + c2*v**3 + c3*v + c4*x + c5 + c6*cos(c7*t + c8)`

- The GT has `v*exp(-|v|)` which cannot be represented by these basis functions.

**Candidate 11:** `c0*x**3 + c1*x**2 + c2*x + c3 + c4*cos(c5*t + c6) + c7*v*x**2 + c8*v*Abs(v) + c9*v*Abs(v)**2`

**Candidate 12:** `c0 + c1*exp(c2*x) + c3*sin(c4*t + c5) + c6*v*Abs(v)`
